# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes API Server Authentication Chain

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement API server authentication: the authenticator chain construction, the bearer token authenticator, the client certificate authenticator, the service account token authenticator, and the anonymous authenticator.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

REQUEST AUTHENTICATORS - These process HTTP requests directly:\\n   - The request union authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/union/union.go) chains multiple request authenticators\\n   - Front-proxy/header-based authenticator (headerrequest) for front proxy scenarios\\n   - Client certificate (x509) authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/x509/x509.go) - verifies client certificates and extracts user info from CommonName and Organization\\n   - Bearer token authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/bearertoken/bearertoken.go) - extracts bearer tokens from Authorization header\\n   - WebSocket protocol authenticator for WebSocket upgrades\\n   - Anonymous authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/anonymous/anonymous.go) - allows unauthenticated access as system:anonymous user\\n\\n2. TOKEN AUTHENTICATORS - These verify extracted bearer tokens:\\n   - Token file authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/token/tokenfile/tokenfile.go) - verifies tokens from a CSV file\\n   - Service account JWT authenticator (pkg/serviceaccount/jwt.go) - verifies Kubernetes service account tokens using JWT validation\\n   - Bootstrap token authenticator (plugin/pkg/auth/authenticator/token/bootstrap/bootstrap.go) - handles cluster bootstrap tokens from kube-system namespace\\n   - Webhook token authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/plugin/pkg/authenticator/token/webhook/webhook.go) - delegates token verification to a webhook server\\n   - Token caching authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/token/cache/cache.go) - caches authentication results\\n\\nThe complete chain construction flow in Config.New() is:\\n1. Request authenticators are added first: front-proxy header authenticator, then client certificates\\n2. Token authenticators are combined into a union via tokenunion.New()\\n3. REQUEST AUTHENTICATORS - These process HTTP requests directly:\\n   - The request union authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/union/union.go) chains multiple request authenticators\\n   - Front-proxy/header-based authenticator (headerrequest) for front proxy scenarios\\n   - Client certificate (x509) authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/x509/x509.go) - verifies client certificates and extracts user info from CommonName and Organization\\n   - Bearer token authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/bearertoken/bearertoken.go) - extracts bearer tokens from Authorization header\\n   - WebSocket protocol authenticator for WebSocket upgrades\\n   - Anonymous authenticator (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/request/anonymous/anonymous.go) - allows unauthenticated access as system:anonymous user\\n\\n2. Request authenticators are added first: front-proxy header authenticator, then client certificates\\n2. Token authenticators are combined into a union via tokenunion.New()\\n3. The token union is wrapped with caching if configured\\n4. Bearer token request authenticator wraps the token union to extract and verify bearer tokens\\n5. The request authenticators union (union.New()) combines all request authenticators\\n6. AuthenticatedGroupAdder wraps the chain to add system:authenticated group to successful authentications\\n7. Finally, the anonymous authenticator is added as a fallback using NewFailOnError() to handle unauthenticated requests\\n\\nThe delegating authenticator factory (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authentication/authenticatorfactory/delegating.go) provides a similar but simpler chain for non-API-server components that need to verify tokens against the API server.\\n\\nKey architectural decisions:\\n- The union authenticators (both request and token level) try each authenticator in sequence until one succeeds\\n- NewFailOnError() versions of union authenticators stop on first error rather than trying all options\\n- Caching is applied to avoid repeated authentication work for tokens\\n- The anonymous authenticator uses NewFailOnError() to ensure no actual authentication method falls back to anonymous\\n- Request-level authenticators handle different protocol variations (HTTP, WebSocket)\\n- Token-level authenticators handle different token formats (CSV, JWT, bootstrap tokens, webhook)\"\n}\n",
